I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[navigation menu] Support inlined nesting
# Bug report

## Current behavior

### 1. `--popup-height` is not updated on content change

When the content inside `NavigationMenu.Content` changes (e.g. dynamically loaded or conditionally rendered), the `--popup-height` variable is not updated to reflect the new height. As a result, if you're animating the popup height using this variable, the transition breaks — the height appears stuck at its previous value (`auto`), and no animation occurs. The only way to update it is by activating another trigger, which forces a re-evaluation, but nothing listens to content size changes dynamically.

### 2. No transition on nested NavigationMenu

When nesting another `NavigationMenu` inside a parent item (e.g. for multi-level navigation), and using a `defaultValue` to preselect a nested item, the transition effect is skipped entirely. It seems like the inner `NavigationMenu.Viewport` is delayed in rendering or measuring, and that causes the quick jump instead of a smooth transition.

### 3. No direction-based transitions when skipping `Positioner`/`Popover`

Migrating from Radix UI's `NavigationMenu`, we had the ability to render the `Viewport` without a `Portal`, `Positioner`, or `Popover`. This was useful for building custom layouts like nested menus without extra wrappers.

With Base UI's current setup, skipping `Positioner` or `Popover` breaks direction-based transitions. The `Content` seems unaware of the "activation direction" (`left | right | top | bottom`), so the enter animation doesn't apply. It seems necessary to wrap everything again inside `Positioner`/`Popover`, even if it's not needed visually, just to get the state propagation working.

## Expected behavior

- The `--popup-height` CSS variable should update reactively when content height changes, enabling smooth transitions.
- Nested `NavigationMenu` transitions should respect the correct enter/exit animations when `defaultValue` is set.
- `NavigationMenu.Content` should still be able to determine the activation direction and animate correctly even if `Popover`/`Positioner` are not used, to support more flexible layout use cases.

## Reproducible example

https://stackblitz.com/edit/vitejs-vite-4erpxnu7?file=src%2FApp.tsx

## Base UI version

1.0.0-beta.1

## Which browser are you using?

Chrome (latest version)

## Which OS are you using?

macOS

## Which assistive tech are you using (if applicable)?

N/A

   212	
   213	  const { open } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
   214	
   215	  const state: NavigationMenuRoot.State = React.useMemo(
   216	    () => ({
   217	      open,
   218	      nested,
   219	    }),
   220	    [open, nested],
   221	  );
   222

   224	    state,
   225	    ref: [props.forwardedRef, rootRef],
   226	    props: [{ 'aria-orientation': orientation }, elementProps],
   227	  });
   228	
   229	  return (
   230	    <NavigationMenuTreeContext.Provider value={nodeId}>
   231	      {element}
   232	    </NavigationMenuTreeContext.Provider>
   233	  );

   237	  export interface State {
   238	    /**
   239	     * If `true`, the popup is open.
   240	     */
   241	    open: boolean;
   242	    /**
   243	     * Whether the navigation menu is nested.
   244	     */
   245	    nested: boolean;
   246	  }
   247	
   248	  export interface Props extends BaseUIComponentProps<'nav', State> {
   249	    /**
   250	     * A ref to imperative actions.
   251	     */
   252	    actionsRef?: React.RefObject<Actions>;
   253	    /**
   254	     * Event handler called after any animations complete when the navigation menu is closed.
   255	     */
   256	    onOpenChangeComplete?: (open: boolean) => void;
   257	    /**
   258	     * The controlled value of the navigation menu item that should be currently open.
   259	     * When non-nullish, the menu will be open. When nullish, the menu will be closed.
   260	     *
   261	     * To render an uncontrolled navigation menu, use the `defaultValue` prop instead.
   262	     * @default null
   263	     */
   264	    value?: any;
   265	    /**
   266	     * The uncontrolled value of the item that should be initially selected.
   267	     *
   268	     * To render a controlled navigation menu, use the `value` prop instead.
   269	     * @default null
   270	     */
   271	    defaultValue?: any;
   272	    /**
   273	     * Callback fired when the value changes.
   274	     */
   275	    onValueChange?: (
   276	      value: any,
   277	      event: Event | undefined,
   278	      reason: BaseOpenChangeReason | undefined,
   279	    ) => void;
   280	    /**
   281	     * How long to wait before opening the navigation menu. Specified in milliseconds.
   282	     * @default 50
   283	     */
   284	    delay?: number;
   285	    /**
   286	     * How long to wait before closing the navigation menu. Specified in milliseconds.
   287	     * @default 50
   288	     */
   289	    closeDelay?: number;
   290	    /**
   291	     * The orientation of the navigation menu.
   292	     * @default 'horizontal'
   293	     */
   294	    orientation?: 'horizontal' | 'vertical';
   295	  }
   296	
   297	  export interface Actions {
   298	    /**
   299	     * When specified, the navigation menu will not be unmounted when closed.
   300	     * Instead, the `unmount` function must be called to unmount the navigation menu manually.
   301	     * Useful when the navigation menu's animation is controlled by an external library.
   302	     */
   303	    unmount: () => void;
   304	  }
   305	}

     8	} from '../../floating-ui-react/utils';

    16	import { useNavigationMenuPositionerContext } from '../positioner/NavigationMenuPositionerContext';
    17	import { useDirection } from '../../direction-provider/DirectionContext';
    18	import { CustomStyleHookMapping } from '../../utils/getStyleHookProps';
    19	import { popupStateMapping as baseMapping } from '../../utils/popupStateMapping';
    20	
    21	const customStyleHookMapping: CustomStyleHookMapping<NavigationMenuPopup.State> = {
    22	  ...baseMapping,
    23	  ...transitionStatusMapping,
    24	};
    25	
    26	/**
    27	 * A container for the navigation menu contents.
    28	 * Renders a `<nav>` element.
    29	 *
    30	 * Documentation: [Base UI Navigation Menu](https://base-ui.com/react/components/navigation-menu)
    31	 */
    32	export const NavigationMenuPopup = React.forwardRef(function NavigationMenuPopup(
    33	  componentProps: NavigationMenuPopup.Props,
    34	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<HTMLElement>,
    35	) {
    36	  const { className, render, id: idProp, ...elementProps } = componentProps;
    37	
    38	  const {
    39	    open,
    40	    transitionStatus,
    41	    popupElement,
    42	    positionerElement,
    43	    setPopupElement,
    44	    beforeInsideRef,
    45	    beforeOutsideRef,
    46	    afterInsideRef,
    47	    afterOutsideRef,
    48	  } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
    49	  const positioning = useNavigationMenuPositionerContext();
    50	  const direction = useDirection();
    51	
    52	  const id = useBaseUiId(idProp);
    53	
    54	  const state: NavigationMenuPopup.State = React.useMemo(
    55	    () => ({
    56	      open,
    57	      transitionStatus,
    58	      side: positioning.side,
    59	      align: positioning.align,
    60	      anchorHidden: positioning.anchorHidden,
    61	    }),
    62	    [open, transitionStatus, positioning.side, positioning.align, positioning.anchorHidden],
    63	  );
    64	
    65	  // Allow the arrow to transition while the popup's size transitions.
    66	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
    67	    if (!popupElement || typeof ResizeObserver === 'undefined') {
    68	      return undefined;
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    const observer = new ResizeObserver(positioning.update);
    72	    observer.observe(popupElement);
    73	    return () => {
    74	      observer.disconnect();
    75	    };
    76	  }, [popupElement, positioning.update]);
    77	
    78	  // Ensure popup size transitions correctly when anchored to `bottom` (side=top) or `right` (side=left).
    79	  let isOriginSide = positioning.side === 'top';
    80	  let isPhysicalLeft = positioning.side === 'left';
    81	  if (direction === 'rtl') {
    82	    isOriginSide = isOriginSide || positioning.side === 'inline-end';
    83	    isPhysicalLeft = isPhysicalLeft || positioning.side === 'inline-end';
    84	  } else {
    85	    isOriginSide = isOriginSide || positioning.side === 'inline-start';
    86	    isPhysicalLeft = isPhysicalLeft || positioning.side === 'inline-start';
    87	  }
    88	
    89	  const element = useRenderElement('nav', componentProps, {
    90	    state,
    91	    ref: [forwardedRef, setPopupElement],
    92	    props: [
    93	      {
    94	        id,
    95	        tabIndex: -1,
    96	        style: isOriginSide
    97	          ? {
    98	              position: 'absolute',
    99	              [positioning.side === 'top' ? 'bottom' : 'top']: '0',
   100	              [isPhysicalLeft ? 'right' : 'left']: '0',
   101	            }
   102	          : {},
   103	      },
   104	      elementProps,
   105	    ],
   106	    customStyleHookMapping,
   107	  });
   108	
   109	  return (
   110	    <React.Fragment>
   111	      <FocusGuard
   112	        ref={beforeInsideRef}
   113	        onFocus={(event) => {
   114	          if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   115	            getNextTabbable(positionerElement)?.focus();
   116	          } else {
   117	            beforeOutsideRef.current?.focus();
   118	          }
   119	        }}
   120	      />
   121	      {element}
   122	      <FocusGuard
   123	        ref={afterInsideRef}
   124	        onFocus={(event) => {
   125	          if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   126	            getPreviousTabbable(positionerElement)?.focus();
   127	          } else {
   128	            afterOutsideRef.current?.focus();
   129	          }
   130	        }}
   131	      />
   132	    </React.Fragment>
   133	  );
   134	});

   140	     */
   141	    open: boolean;
   142	    /**

   144	     */
   145	    transitionStatus: TransitionStatus;
   146	  }

   149	}

     7	import {
     8	  disableFocusInside,
     9	  enableFocusInside,
    10	  isOutsideEvent,
    11	} from '../../floating-ui-react/utils';

    25	const adaptiveOrigin: Middleware = {
    26	  name: 'adaptiveOrigin',
    27	  async fn(state) {
    28	    const {
    29	      x: rawX,
    30	      y: rawY,
    31	      rects: { floating: floatRect },
    32	      elements: { floating },
    33	      platform,
    34	      strategy,
    35	      placement,
    36	    } = state;
    37	
    38	    const win = floating.ownerDocument.defaultView;
    39	    const offsetParent = await platform.getOffsetParent?.(floating);
    40	
    41	    let offsetDimensions = { width: 0, height: 0 };
    42	
    43	    // For fixed strategy, prefer visualViewport if available
    44	    if (strategy === 'fixed' && win?.visualViewport) {
    45	      offsetDimensions = {
    46	        width: win.visualViewport.width,
    47	        height: win.visualViewport.height,
    48	      };
    49	    } else if (offsetParent === win) {
    50	      const doc = ownerDocument(floating);
    51	      offsetDimensions = {
    52	        width: doc.documentElement.clientWidth,
    53	        height: doc.documentElement.clientHeight,
    54	      };
    55	    } else if (await platform.isElement?.(offsetParent)) {
    56	      offsetDimensions = await platform.getDimensions(offsetParent);
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    const currentSide = getSide(placement);
    60	    let x = rawX;
    61	    let y = rawY;
    62	
    63	    if (currentSide === 'left') {
    64	      x = offsetDimensions.width - (rawX + floatRect.width);
    65	    }
    66	    if (currentSide === 'top') {
    67	      y = offsetDimensions.height - (rawY + floatRect.height);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    const sideX = currentSide === 'left' ? 'right' : 'left';
    71	    const sideY = currentSide === 'top' ? 'bottom' : 'top';
    72	    return {
    73	      x,
    74	      y,
    75	      data: {
    76	        sideX,
    77	        sideY,
    78	      },
    79	    };
    80	  },
    81	};

    83	/**
    84	 * Positions the navigation menu against the currently active trigger.
    85	 * Renders a `<div>` element.
    86	 *
    87	 * Documentation: [Base UI Navigation Menu](https://base-ui.com/react/components/navigation-menu)
    88	 */
    89	export const NavigationMenuPositioner = React.forwardRef(function NavigationMenuPositioner(
    90	  componentProps: NavigationMenuPositioner.Props,
    91	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<HTMLDivElement>,
    92	) {
    93	  const { open, mounted, positionerElement, setPositionerElement, floatingRootContext, nested } =
    94	    useNavigationMenuRootContext();
    95	
    96	  const {
    97	    className,
    98	    render,
    99	    anchor,
   100	    positionMethod = 'absolute',
   101	    side = 'bottom',
   102	    align = 'center',
   103	    sideOffset = 0,
   104	    alignOffset = 0,
   105	    collisionBoundary = 'clipping-ancestors',
   106	    collisionPadding = 5,
   107	    collisionAvoidance = nested ? POPUP_COLLISION_AVOIDANCE : DROPDOWN_COLLISION_AVOIDANCE,
   108	    arrowPadding = 5,
   109	    sticky = false,
   110	    trackAnchor = true,
   111	    ...elementProps
   112	  } = componentProps;
   113	
   114	  const keepMounted = useNavigationMenuPortalContext();
   115	  const nodeId = useNavigationMenuTreeContext();
   116	
   117	  const [instant, setInstant] = React.useState(true);
   118	
   119	  const positionerRef = React.useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
   120	  const prevTriggerElementRef = React.useRef<Element | null>(null);
   121	
   122	  const runOnceAnimationsFinish = useAnimationsFinished(positionerRef);
   123	
   124	  // When the current trigger element changes, enable transitions on the
   125	  // positioner temporarily
   126	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
   127	    const currentTriggerElement = floatingRootContext?.elements.domReference;
   128	    const prevTriggerElement = prevTriggerElementRef.current;
   129	
   130	    if (currentTriggerElement) {
   131	      prevTriggerElementRef.current = currentTriggerElement;
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    if (
   135	      prevTriggerElement &&
   136	      currentTriggerElement &&
   137	      currentTriggerElement !== prevTriggerElement
   138	    ) {
   139	      setInstant(false);
   140	      const ac = new AbortController();
   141	      runOnceAnimationsFinish(() => {
   142	        setInstant(true);
   143	      }, ac.signal);
   144	      return () => {
   145	        ac.abort();
   146	      };
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    return undefined;
   150	  }, [floatingRootContext?.elements.domReference, runOnceAnimationsFinish]);
   151	
   152	  // https://codesandbox.io/s/tabbable-portal-f4tng?file=/src/TabbablePortal.tsx
   153	  React.useEffect(() => {
   154	    if (!positionerElement) {
   155	      return undefined;
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    // Make sure elements inside the portal element are tabbable only when the
   159	    // portal has already been focused, either by tabbing into a focus trap
   160	    // element outside or using the mouse.
   161	    function onFocus(event: FocusEvent) {
   162	      if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event)) {
   163	        const focusing = event.type === 'focusin';
   164	        const manageFocus = focusing ? enableFocusInside : disableFocusInside;
   165	        manageFocus(positionerElement);
   166	      }
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    // Listen to the event on the capture phase so they run before the focus
   170	    // trap elements onFocus prop is called.
   171	    positionerElement.addEventListener('focusin', onFocus, true);
   172	    positionerElement.addEventListener('focusout', onFocus, true);
   173	    return () => {
   174	      positionerElement.removeEventListener('focusin', onFocus, true);
   175	      positionerElement.removeEventListener('focusout', onFocus, true);
   176	    };
   177	  }, [positionerElement]);
   178	
   179	  const positioning = useAnchorPositioning({
   180	    anchor: anchor ?? floatingRootContext?.elements.domReference ?? prevTriggerElementRef,
   181	    positionMethod,
   182	    mounted,
   183	    side,
   184	    sideOffset,
   185	    align,
   186	    alignOffset,
   187	    arrowPadding,
   188	    collisionBoundary,
   189	    collisionPadding,
   190	    sticky,
   191	    trackAnchor,
   192	    keepMounted,
   193	    floatingRootContext,
   194	    collisionAvoidance,
   195	    nodeId,
   196	    // Allows the menu to remain anchored without wobbling while its size
   197	    // and position transition simultaneously when side=top or side=left.
   198	    adaptiveOrigin,
   199	  });
   200	
   201	  const defaultProps: React.ComponentProps<'div'> = React.useMemo(() => {
   202	    const hiddenStyles: React.CSSProperties = {};
   203	
   204	    if (!open) {
   205	      hiddenStyles.pointerEvents = 'none';
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    return {
   209	      role: 'presentation',
   210	      hidden: !mounted,
   211	      style: {
   212	        ...positioning.positionerStyles,
   213	        ...hiddenStyles,
   214	      },
   215	    };
   216	  }, [open, mounted, positioning.positionerStyles]);
   217	
   218	  const state: NavigationMenuPositioner.State = React.useMemo(
   219	    () => ({
   220	      open,
   221	      side: positioning.side,
   222	      align: positioning.align,
   223	      anchorHidden: positioning.anchorHidden,
   224	      instant,
   225	    }),
   226	    [open, positioning.side, positioning.align, positioning.anchorHidden, instant],
   227	  );
   228	
   229	  const element = useRenderElement('div', componentProps, {
   230	    state,
   231	    ref: [forwardedRef, setPositionerElement, positionerRef],
   232	    props: [defaultProps, elementProps],
   233	    customStyleHookMapping: popupStateMapping,
   234	  });
   235	
   236	  return (
   237	    <NavigationMenuPositionerContext.Provider value={positioning}>
   238	      {element}
   239	    </NavigationMenuPositionerContext.Provider>
   240	  );
   241	});
   242	
   243	export namespace NavigationMenuPositioner {
   244	  export interface State {
   245	    /**
   246	     * Whether the navigation menu is currently open.
   247	     */
   248	    open: boolean;
   249	    side: Side;
   250	    align: Align;
   251	    anchorHidden: boolean;
   252	    /**
   253	     * Whether CSS transitions should be disabled.
   254	     */
   255	    instant: boolean;
   256	  }
   257	
   258	  export interface Props
   259	    extends useAnchorPositioning.SharedParameters,
   260	      BaseUIComponentProps<'div', State> {}
   261	}

    33	/**
    34	 * A container for the content of the navigation menu item that is moved into the popup
    35	 * when the item is active.
    36	 * Renders a `<div>` element.
    37	 *
    38	 * Documentation: [Base UI Navigation Menu](https://base-ui.com/react/components/navigation-menu)
    39	 */
    40	export const NavigationMenuContent = React.forwardRef(function NavigationMenuContent(
    41	  componentProps: NavigationMenuContent.Props,
    42	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<HTMLDivElement>,
    43	) {
    44	  const { className, render, ...elementProps } = componentProps;
    45	
    46	  const {
    47	    mounted: popupMounted,
    48	    viewportElement,
    49	    value,
    50	    activationDirection,
    51	    currentContentRef,
    52	  } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
    53	  const itemValue = useNavigationMenuItemContext();
    54	  const nodeId = useNavigationMenuTreeContext();
    55	
    56	  const open = popupMounted && value === itemValue;
    57	
    58	  const ref = React.useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
    59	
    60	  const [focusInside, setFocusInside] = React.useState(false);
    61	
    62	  const { mounted, setMounted, transitionStatus } = useTransitionStatus(open);
    63	
    64	  useOpenChangeComplete({
    65	    ref,
    66	    open,
    67	    onComplete() {
    68	      if (!open) {
    69	        setMounted(false);
    70	      }
    71	    },
    72	  });
    73	
    74	  const state: NavigationMenuContent.State = React.useMemo(
    75	    () => ({
    76	      open,
    77	      transitionStatus,
    78	      activationDirection,
    79	    }),
    80	    [open, transitionStatus, activationDirection],
    81	  );
    82	
    83	  const handleCurrentContentRef = React.useCallback(
    84	    (node: HTMLDivElement | null) => {
    85	      if (node) {
    86	        currentContentRef.current = node;
    87	      }
    88	    },
    89	    [currentContentRef],
    90	  );
    91	
    92	  const commonProps: HTMLProps = {
    93	    onFocus() {
    94	      setFocusInside(true);
    95	    },
    96	    onBlur(event) {
    97	      if (!contains(event.currentTarget, event.relatedTarget)) {
    98	        setFocusInside(false);
    99	      }
   100	    },
   101	  };
   102	
   103	  const defaultProps: HTMLProps =
   104	    !open && mounted
   105	      ? {
   106	          style: { position: 'absolute', top: 0, left: 0 },
   107	          inert: inertValue(!focusInside),
   108	          ...commonProps,
   109	        }
   110	      : commonProps;
   111	
   112	  const shouldRender = viewportElement !== null && mounted;
   113	
   114	  if (!viewportElement || !shouldRender) {
   115	    return null;
   116	  }
   117	
   118	  return ReactDOM.createPortal(
   119	    <FloatingNode id={nodeId}>
   120	      <CompositeRoot
   121	        render={render}
   122	        className={className}
   123	        state={state}
   124	        refs={[forwardedRef, ref, handleCurrentContentRef]}
   125	        props={[defaultProps, elementProps]}
   126	        customStyleHookMapping={customStyleHookMapping}
   127	        stopEventPropagation
   128	      />
   129	    </FloatingNode>,
   130	    viewportElement,
   131	  );
   132	});

   143	    transitionStatus: TransitionStatus;

   147	    activationDirection: 'left' | 'right' | 'up' | 'down' | null;

    47	function useNavigationMenuRootContext(optional?: boolean) {
    48	  const context = React.useContext(NavigationMenuRootContext);

    87	  const sizeFrame1 = useAnimationFrame();
    88	  const sizeFrame2 = useAnimationFrame();

    90	  const [triggerElement, setTriggerElement] = React.useState<HTMLElement | null>(null);
    91	  const [stickIfOpen, setStickIfOpen] = React.useState(true);
    92	  const [pointerType, setPointerType] = React.useState<'mouse' | 'touch' | 'pen' | ''>('');
    93	
    94	  const isActiveItem = open && value === itemValue;
    95	  const isActiveItemRef = useLatestRef(isActiveItem);
    96	
    97	  const allowFocusRef = React.useRef(false);
    98	
    99	  const handleValueChange = useEventCallback((currentWidth: number, currentHeight: number) => {
   100	    if (!popupElement || !positionerElement) {
   101	      return;
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    popupElement.style.removeProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupWidth);
   105	    popupElement.style.removeProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupHeight);
   106	    positionerElement.style.removeProperty(NavigationMenuPositionerCssVars.positionerWidth);
   107	    positionerElement.style.removeProperty(NavigationMenuPositionerCssVars.positionerHeight);
   108	
   109	    const nextWidth = popupElement.offsetWidth;
   110	    const nextHeight = popupElement.offsetHeight;
   111	
   112	    if (currentHeight === 0 || currentWidth === 0) {
   113	      currentWidth = nextWidth;
   114	      currentHeight = nextHeight;
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    popupElement.style.setProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupWidth, `${currentWidth}px`);
   118	    popupElement.style.setProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupHeight, `${currentHeight}px`);
   119	    positionerElement.style.setProperty(

   131	        popupElement.style.setProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupHeight, `${nextHeight}px`);
   132	      });
   133	    });
   134	  });
   135

   137	    if (!popupElement) {
   138	      return;

   141	    popupElement.style.setProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupWidth, 'auto');

   147	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
   148	    if (!positionerElement || !popupElement || !open) {
   149	      return undefined;
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    sizeFrame1.request(() => {
   153	      sizeFrame2.request(setAutoSizes);
   154	    });

   157	      sizeFrame2.cancel();

   163	      return undefined;
   164	    }

   168	      sizeFrame2.request(() => {
   169	        runOnceAnimationsFinish(setAutoSizes, ac.signal);

   171	    });

   174	      sizeFrame1.cancel();
   175	      sizeFrame2.cancel();

   179	    value,
   180	    popupElement,
   181	    positionerElement,
   182	    runOnceAnimationsFinish,
   183	    sizeFrame1,
   184	    sizeFrame2,
   185	    setAutoSizes,
   186	  ]);

   189	    if (!open) {
   190	      setPointerType('');
   191	      stickIfOpenTimeout.clear();
   192	      sizeFrame1.cancel();
   193	      sizeFrame2.cancel();
   194	    }

   206	      focusFrame.request(() => {

   210	
   211	    return () => {
   212	      focusFrame.cancel();
   213	    };
   214	  }, [beforeOutsideRef, focusFrame, handleValueChange, isActiveItem, open, popupElement]);
   215	
   216	  function handleOpenChange(
   217	    nextOpen: boolean,
   218	    event: Event | undefined,
   219	    reason: BaseOpenChangeReason | undefined,
   220	  ) {
   221	    const isHover = reason === 'trigger-hover';
   222	
   223	    if (pointerType === 'touch' && isHover) {
   224	      return;
   225	    }
   226	
   227	    if (!nextOpen && value !== itemValue) {
   228	      return;
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    if (!nextOpen && popupElement && positionerElement) {
   232	      popupElement.style.setProperty(
   233	        NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupWidth,
   234	        `${popupElement.offsetWidth}px`,
   235	      );
   236	      popupElement.style.setProperty(
   237	        NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupHeight,
   238	        `${popupElement.offsetHeight}px`,
   239	      );
   240	      positionerElement.style.setProperty(
   241	        NavigationMenuPositionerCssVars.positionerWidth,
   242	        `${positionerElement.offsetWidth}px`,
   243	      );
   244	      positionerElement.style.setProperty(
   245	        NavigationMenuPositionerCssVars.positionerHeight,
   246	        `${positionerElement.offsetHeight}px`,
   247	      );
   248	    }
   249	
   250	    function changeState() {
   251	      if (isHover) {
   252	        // Only allow "patient" clicks to close the popup if it's open.
   253	        // If they clicked within 500ms of the popup opening, keep it open.
   254	        setStickIfOpen(true);
   255	        stickIfOpenTimeout.clear();
   256	        stickIfOpenTimeout.start(PATIENT_CLICK_THRESHOLD, () => {
   257	          setStickIfOpen(false);
   258	        });
   259	      }
   260	
   261	      if (nextOpen) {
   262	        setValue(itemValue, event, reason);
   263	      } else {
   264	        setValue(null, event, reason);
   265	      }
   266	    }
   267	
   268	    if (isHover) {
   269	      ReactDOM.flushSync(changeState);
   270	    } else {
   271	      changeState();
   272	    }
   273	  }
   274	
   275	  const context = useFloatingRootContext({
   276	    open,
   277	    onOpenChange(openValue, eventValue, reasonValue) {
   278	      handleOpenChange(openValue, eventValue, translateOpenChangeReason(reasonValue));
   279	    },
   280	    elements: {
   281	      reference: triggerElement,
   282	      floating: positionerElement,
   283	    },
   284	  });
   285	
   286	  const hover = useHover(context, {
   287	    move: false,
   288	    handleClose: safePolygon({ blockPointerEvents: pointerType !== 'touch' }),
   289	    restMs: mounted ? 0 : delay,
   290	    delay: { close: closeDelay },
   291	  });
   292	  const click = useClick(context, {
   293	    stickIfOpen,
   294	    toggle: isActiveItem,
   295	  });
   296	  const dismiss = useDismiss(context, {
   297	    enabled: isActiveItem,
   298	    outsidePress(event) {
   299	      // When pressing a new trigger with touch input, prevent closing the popup.
   300	      const target = getTarget(event) as HTMLElement | null;
   301	      const closestNavigationMenuTrigger = target?.closest(`[${TRIGGER_IDENTIFIER}]`);
   302	      return closestNavigationMenuTrigger === null;
   303	    },
   304	  });
   305	
   306	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
   307	    if (isActiveItem) {
   308	      setFloatingRootContext(context);
   309	      prevTriggerElementRef.current = triggerElement;
   310	    }
   311	  }, [isActiveItem, context, setFloatingRootContext, prevTriggerElementRef, triggerElement]);
   312	
   313	  const { getReferenceProps } = useInteractions([hover, click, dismiss]);
   314	
   315	  const handleOpenEvent = useEventCallback((event: React.MouseEvent | React.KeyboardEvent) => {
   316	    if (!popupElement || !positionerElement) {
   317	      return;
   318	    }
   319	
   320	    const currentWidth = popupElement.offsetWidth;
   321	    const currentHeight = popupElement.offsetHeight;
   322	
   323	    ReactDOM.flushSync(() => {
   324	      const prevTriggerRect = prevTriggerElementRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
   325	
   326	      if (mounted && prevTriggerRect && triggerElement) {
   327	        const nextTriggerRect = triggerElement.getBoundingClientRect();
   328	        const isMovingRight = nextTriggerRect.left > prevTriggerRect.left;
   329	        const isMovingDown = nextTriggerRect.top > prevTriggerRect.top;
   330	
   331	        if (orientation === 'horizontal' && nextTriggerRect.left !== prevTriggerRect.left) {
   332	          setActivationDirection(isMovingRight ? 'right' : 'left');
   333	        } else if (orientation === 'vertical' && nextTriggerRect.top !== prevTriggerRect.top) {
   334	          setActivationDirection(isMovingDown ? 'down' : 'up');
   335	        }
   336	      }
   337	
   338	      // Reset the `openEvent` to `undefined` when the active item changes so that a
   339	      // `click` -> `hover` on new trigger -> `hover` back to old trigger doesn't unexpectedly
   340	      // cause the popup to remain stuck open when leaving the old trigger.
   341	      if (event.type !== 'click') {
   342	        context.dataRef.current.openEvent = undefined;
   343	      }
   344	
   345	      if (pointerType === 'touch' && event.type !== 'click') {
   346	        return;
   347	      }
   348	
   349	      if (value != null) {
   350	        setValue(
   351	          itemValue,
   352	          event.nativeEvent,
   353	          event.type === 'mouseenter' ? 'trigger-hover' : 'trigger-press',
   354	        );
   355	      }
   356	    });
   357	
   358	    handleValueChange(currentWidth, currentHeight);
   359	  });
   360	
   361	  const state: NavigationMenuTrigger.State = React.useMemo(
   362	    () => ({
   363	      open: isActiveItem,
   364	    }),
   365	    [isActiveItem],
   366	  );
   367	
   368	  function handleSetPointerType(event: React.PointerEvent) {
   369	    setPointerType(event.pointerType);
   370	  }
   371	
   372	  const defaultProps: HTMLProps = {
   373	    tabIndex: 0,
   374	    onMouseEnter: handleOpenEvent,
   375	    onClick: handleOpenEvent,
   376	    onPointerEnter: handleSetPointerType,
   377	    onPointerDown: handleSetPointerType,
   378	    'aria-expanded': isActiveItem,
   379	    'aria-controls': isActiveItem ? popupElement?.id : undefined,
   380	    [TRIGGER_IDENTIFIER as string]: '',
   381	    onMouseMove() {
   382	      allowFocusRef.current = false;
   383	    },
   384	    onKeyDown(event) {
   385	      allowFocusRef.current = true;
   386	      const openHorizontal = orientation === 'horizontal' && event.key === 'ArrowDown';
   387	      const openVertical = orientation === 'vertical' && event.key === 'ArrowRight';
   388	
   389	      if (openHorizontal || openVertical) {
   390	        setValue(itemValue, event.nativeEvent, 'list-navigation');
   391	        handleOpenEvent(event);
   392	        stopEvent(event);
   393	      }
   394	    },
   395	    onBlur(event) {
   396	      if (
   397	        event.relatedTarget &&
   398	        isOutsideMenuEvent(
   399	          {
   400	            currentTarget: event.currentTarget,
   401	            relatedTarget: event.relatedTarget as HTMLElement | null,
   402	          },
   403	          { popupElement, rootRef, tree, nodeId },
   404	        )
   405	      ) {
   406	        setValue(null, event.nativeEvent, 'focus-out');
   407	      }
   408	    },
   409	  };
   410	
   411	  const { getButtonProps, buttonRef } = useButton({
   412	    disabled,
   413	    focusableWhenDisabled: true,
   414	    native: nativeButton,
   415	  });
   416	
   417	  return (
   418	    <React.Fragment>
   419	      <CompositeItem
   420	        tag="button"
   421	        render={render}
   422	        className={className}
   423	        state={state}
   424	        customStyleHookMapping={pressableTriggerOpenStateMapping}
   425	        refs={[forwardedRef, setTriggerElement, buttonRef]}
   426	        props={[getReferenceProps, defaultProps, elementProps, getButtonProps]}
   427	      />
   428	      {isActiveItem && (
   429	        <React.Fragment>
   430	          <FocusGuard
   431	            ref={beforeOutsideRef}
   432	            onFocus={(event) => {
   433	              if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   434	                beforeInsideRef.current?.focus();
   435	              } else {
   436	                const prevTabbable = getPreviousTabbable(triggerElement);
   437	                prevTabbable?.focus();
   438	              }
   439	            }}
   440	          />
   441	          <span aria-owns={popupElement?.id} style={visuallyHidden} />
   442	          <FocusGuard
   443	            ref={afterOutsideRef}
   444	            onFocus={(event) => {
   445	              if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   446	                afterInsideRef.current?.focus();
   447	              } else {
   448	                const nextTabbable = getNextTabbable(triggerElement);
   449	                nextTabbable?.focus();
   450	
   451	                if (!contains(rootRef.current, nextTabbable)) {
   452	                  setValue(null, event.nativeEvent, 'focus-out');
   453	                }
   454	              }
   455	            }}
   456	          />
   457	        </React.Fragment>
   458	      )}
   459	    </React.Fragment>
   460	  );
   461	});
   462	
   463	export namespace NavigationMenuTrigger {
   464	  export interface State {
   465	    /**
   466	     * If `true`, the popup is open and the item is active.
   467	     */
   468	    open: boolean;
   469	  }
   470	
   471	  export interface Props extends NativeButtonProps, BaseUIComponentProps<'button', State> {}
   472	}

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/packages/react/src/utils/useTransitionStatus.ts:
     1	'use client';
     2	import * as React from 'react';
     3	import * as ReactDOM from 'react-dom';
     4	import { useIsoLayoutEffect } from '@base-ui-components/utils/useIsoLayoutEffect';
     5	import { AnimationFrame } from '@base-ui-components/utils/useAnimationFrame';
     6	
     7	export type TransitionStatus = 'starting' | 'ending' | 'idle' | undefined;
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * Provides a status string for CSS animations.
    11	 * @param open - a boolean that determines if the element is open.
    12	 * @param enableIdleState - a boolean that enables the `'idle'` state between `'starting'` and `'ending'`
    13	 */
    14	export function useTransitionStatus(
    15	  open: boolean,
    16	  enableIdleState: boolean = false,
    17	  deferEndingState: boolean = false,
    18	) {
    19	  const [transitionStatus, setTransitionStatus] = React.useState<TransitionStatus>(
    20	    open && enableIdleState ? 'idle' : undefined,
    21	  );
    22	  const [mounted, setMounted] = React.useState(open);
    23	
    24	  if (open && !mounted) {
    25	    setMounted(true);
    26	    setTransitionStatus('starting');
    27	  }
    28	
    29	  if (!open && mounted && transitionStatus !== 'ending' && !deferEndingState) {
    30	    setTransitionStatus('ending');
    31	  }
    32	
    33	  if (!open && !mounted && transitionStatus === 'ending') {
    34	    setTransitionStatus(undefined);
    35	  }
    36	
    37	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
    38	    if (!open && mounted && transitionStatus !== 'ending' && deferEndingState) {
    39	      const frame = AnimationFrame.request(() => {
    40	        setTransitionStatus('ending');
    41	      });
    42	
    43	      return () => {
    44	        AnimationFrame.cancel(frame);
    45	      };
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    return undefined;
    49	  }, [open, mounted, transitionStatus, deferEndingState]);
    50	
    51	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
    52	    if (!open || enableIdleState) {
    53	      return undefined;
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    const frame = AnimationFrame.request(() => {
    57	      ReactDOM.flushSync(() => {
    58	        setTransitionStatus(undefined);
    59	      });
    60	    });
    61	
    62	    return () => {
    63	      AnimationFrame.cancel(frame);
    64	    };
    65	  }, [enableIdleState, open]);
    66	
    67	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
    68	    if (!open || !enableIdleState) {
    69	      return undefined;
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    if (open && mounted && transitionStatus !== 'idle') {
    73	      setTransitionStatus('starting');
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    const frame = AnimationFrame.request(() => {
    77	      setTransitionStatus('idle');
    78	    });
    79	
    80	    return () => {
    81	      AnimationFrame.cancel(frame);
    82	    };
    83	  }, [enableIdleState, open, mounted, setTransitionStatus, transitionStatus]);
    84	
    85	  return React.useMemo(
    86	    () => ({
    87	      mounted,
    88	      setMounted,
    89	      transitionStatus,
    90	    }),
    91	    [mounted, transitionStatus],
    92	  );
    93	}
    94

     1	'use client';
     2	import * as React from 'react';
     3	import type { BaseUIComponentProps } from '../../utils/types';
     4	import { useRenderElement } from '../../utils/useRenderElement';
     5	import { NavigationMenuItemContext } from './NavigationMenuItemContext';
     6	import { useBaseUiId } from '../../utils/useBaseUiId';
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * An individual navigation menu item.
    10	 * Renders a `<div>` element.
    11	 *
    12	 * Documentation: [Base UI Navigation Menu](https://base-ui.com/react/components/navigation-menu)
    13	 */
    14	export const NavigationMenuItem = React.forwardRef(function NavigationMenuItem(
    15	  componentProps: NavigationMenuItem.Props,
    16	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<HTMLDivElement>,
    17	) {
    18	  const { className, render, value: valueProp, ...elementProps } = componentProps;
    19	
    20	  const fallbackValue = useBaseUiId();
    21	  const value = valueProp ?? fallbackValue;
    22	
    23	  const element = useRenderElement('div', componentProps, {
    24	    ref: forwardedRef,
    25	    props: elementProps,
    26	  });
    27	
    28	  return (
    29	    <NavigationMenuItemContext.Provider value={value}>{element}</NavigationMenuItemContext.Provider>
    30	  );
    31	});
    32	
    33	export namespace NavigationMenuItem {
    34	  export interface State {}
    35	
    36	  export interface Props extends BaseUIComponentProps<'div', State> {
    37	    /**
    38	     * A unique value that identifies this navigation menu item.
    39	     * If no value is provided, a unique ID will be generated automatically.
    40	     * Use when controlling the navigation menu programmatically.
    41	     */
    42	    value?: any;
    43	  }
    44	}

     1	'use client';
     2	import * as React from 'react';
     3	import { useEventCallback } from '@base-ui-components/utils/useEventCallback';
     4	import { useLatestRef } from '@base-ui-components/utils/useLatestRef';
     5	import { useAnimationsFinished } from './useAnimationsFinished';
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Calls the provided function when the CSS open/close animation or transition completes.
     9	 */
    10	export function useOpenChangeComplete(parameters: useOpenChangeComplete.Parameters) {
    11	  const { enabled = true, open, ref, onComplete: onCompleteParam } = parameters;
    12	
    13	  const openRef = useLatestRef(open);
    14	  const onComplete = useEventCallback(onCompleteParam);
    15	  const runOnceAnimationsFinish = useAnimationsFinished(ref, open);
    16	
    17	  React.useEffect(() => {
    18	    if (!enabled) {
    19	      return;
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    runOnceAnimationsFinish(() => {
    23	      if (open === openRef.current) {
    24	        onComplete();
    25	      }
    26	    });
    27	  }, [enabled, open, onComplete, runOnceAnimationsFinish, openRef]);
    28	}

    32	    /**

    36	    enabled?: boolean;
    37	    /**
    38	     * Whether the element is open.

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/packages/react/src/utils/useAnimationsFinished.ts:
     1	'use client';
     2	import * as React from 'react';
     3	import * as ReactDOM from 'react-dom';
     4	import { useAnimationFrame } from '@base-ui-components/utils/useAnimationFrame';
     5	import { useEventCallback } from '@base-ui-components/utils/useEventCallback';
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Executes a function once all animations have finished on the provided element.
     9	 * @param ref - The element to watch for animations.
    10	 * @param waitForNextTick - Whether to wait for the next tick before checking for animations.
    11	 */
    12	export function useAnimationsFinished(
    13	  ref: React.RefObject<HTMLElement | null>,
    14	  waitForNextTick = false,
    15	) {
    16	  const frame = useAnimationFrame();
    17	
    18	  return useEventCallback(
    19	    (
    20	      /**
    21	       * A function to execute once all animations have finished.
    22	       */
    23	      fnToExecute: () => void,
    24	      /**
    25	       * An optional [AbortSignal](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/AbortSignal) that
    26	       * can be used to abort `fnToExecute` before all the animations have finished.
    27	       * @default null
    28	       */
    29	      signal: AbortSignal | null = null,
    30	    ) => {
    31	      frame.cancel();
    32	
    33	      const element = ref.current;
    34	
    35	      if (!element) {
    36	        return;
    37	      }
    38	
    39	      if (typeof element.getAnimations !== 'function' || globalThis.BASE_UI_ANIMATIONS_DISABLED) {
    40	        fnToExecute();
    41	      } else {
    42	        frame.request(() => {
    43	          function exec() {
    44	            if (!element) {
    45	              return;
    46	            }
    47	
    48	            Promise.allSettled(element.getAnimations().map((anim) => anim.finished)).then(() => {
    49	              if (signal != null && signal.aborted) {
    50	                return;
    51	              }
    52	              // Synchronously flush the unmounting of the component so that the browser doesn't
    53	              // paint: https://github.com/mui/base-ui/issues/979
    54	              ReactDOM.flushSync(fnToExecute);
    55	            });
    56	          }
    57	
    58	          // `open: true` animations need to wait for the next tick to be detected
    59	          if (waitForNextTick) {
    60	            frame.request(exec);
    61	          } else {
    62	            exec();
    63	          }
    64	        });
    65	      }
    66	    },
    67	  );
    68	}
    69

   147	      setViewportElement,
   148	      activationDirection,
   149	      setActivationDirection,
   150	      floatingRootContext,
   151	      setFloatingRootContext,
   152	      currentContentRef,
   153	      isDefaultValue,
   154	      nested,
   155	      rootRef,
   156	      beforeInsideRef,
   157	      afterInsideRef,
   158	      beforeOutsideRef,
   159	      afterOutsideRef,
   160	      prevTriggerElementRef,
   161	      delay,
   162	      closeDelay,
   163	      orientation,
   164	    }),
   165	    [
   166	      open,
   167	      value,
   168	      setValue,
   169	      mounted,
   170	      transitionStatus,
   171	      positionerElement,
   172	      popupElement,
   173	      viewportElement,
   174	      activationDirection,
   175	      floatingRootContext,
   176	      nested,
   177	      delay,
   178	      closeDelay,
   179	      orientation,
   180	    ],
   181	  );
   182	
   183	  const jsx = (
   184	    <NavigationMenuRootContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
   185	      <TreeContext componentProps={componentProps} forwardedRef={forwardedRef}>
   186	        {componentProps.children}
   187	      </TreeContext>
   188	    </NavigationMenuRootContext.Provider>
   189	  );
   190	
   191	  if (!nested) {
   192	    // FloatingTree provides context to nested menus
   193	    return <FloatingTree>{jsx}</FloatingTree>;
   194	  }
   195	
   196	  return jsx;
   197	});
   198	
   199	function TreeContext(props: {
   200	  componentProps: NavigationMenuRoot.Props;
   201	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<HTMLElement>;
   202	  children: React.ReactNode;
   203	}) {
   204	  const {
   205	    className,
   206	    render,
   207	    defaultValue,
   208	    value: valueParam,
   209	    onValueChange,
   210	    actionsRef,
   211	    delay,
   212	    closeDelay,
   213	    orientation,
   214	    onOpenChangeComplete,
   215	    ...elementProps
   216	  } = props.componentProps;
   217	
   218	  const nodeId = useFloatingNodeId();
   219	  const { rootRef, nested } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
   220	
   221	  const { open } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
   222	
   223	  const state: NavigationMenuRoot.State = React.useMemo(
   224	    () => ({
   225	      open,
   226	      nested,
   227	    }),
   228	    [open, nested],
   229	  );
   230	
   231	  const element = useRenderElement(nested ? 'div' : 'nav', props.componentProps, {
   232	    state,
   233	    ref: [props.forwardedRef, rootRef],
   234	    props: [{ 'aria-orientation': orientation }, elementProps],
   235	  });
   236	
   237	  return (
   238	    <NavigationMenuTreeContext.Provider value={nodeId}>
   239	      {element}
   240	    </NavigationMenuTreeContext.Provider>
   241	  );
   242	}
   243	
   244	export namespace NavigationMenuRoot {
   245	  export interface State {
   246	    /**
   247	     * If `true`, the popup is open.
   248	     */
   249	    open: boolean;
   250	    /**
   251	     * Whether the navigation menu is nested.
   252	     */
   253	    nested: boolean;
   254	  }
   255	
   256	  export interface Props extends BaseUIComponentProps<'nav', State> {
   257	    /**
   258	     * A ref to imperative actions.
   259	     */
   260	    actionsRef?: React.RefObject<Actions>;
   261	    /**
   262	     * Event handler called after any animations complete when the navigation menu is closed.
   263	     */
   264	    onOpenChangeComplete?: (open: boolean) => void;
   265	    /**
   266	     * The controlled value of the navigation menu item that should be currently open.
   267	     * When non-nullish, the menu will be open. When nullish, the menu will be closed.
   268	     *
   269	     * To render an uncontrolled navigation menu, use the `defaultValue` prop instead.
   270	     * @default null
   271	     */
   272	    value?: any;
   273	    /**
   274	     * The uncontrolled value of the item that should be initially selected.
   275	     *
   276	     * To render a controlled navigation menu, use the `value` prop instead.
   277	     * @default null
   278	     */
   279	    defaultValue?: any;
   280	    /**
   281	     * Callback fired when the value changes.
   282	     */
   283	    onValueChange?: (
   284	      value: any,
   285	      event: Event | undefined,
   286	      reason: BaseOpenChangeReason | undefined,
   287	    ) => void;
   288	    /**
   289	     * How long to wait before opening the navigation menu. Specified in milliseconds.
   290	     * @default 50
   291	     */
   292	    delay?: number;
   293	    /**
   294	     * How long to wait before closing the navigation menu. Specified in milliseconds.
   295	     * @default 50
   296	     */
   297	    closeDelay?: number;
   298	    /**
   299	     * The orientation of the navigation menu.
   300	     * @default 'horizontal'
   301	     */
   302	    orientation?: 'horizontal' | 'vertical';
   303	  }
   304	
   305	  export interface Actions {
   306	    /**
   307	     * When specified, the navigation menu will not be unmounted when closed.
   308	     * Instead, the `unmount` function must be called to unmount the navigation menu manually.
   309	     * Useful when the navigation menu's animation is controlled by an external library.
   310	     */
   311	    unmount: () => void;
   312	  }
   313	}
   314

   201	function TreeContext(props: {
   202	  componentProps: NavigationMenuRoot.Props;
   203	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<HTMLElement>;
   204	  children: React.ReactNode;
   205	}) {
   206	  const {
   207	    className,
   208	    render,
   209	    defaultValue,

   219	
   220	  const nodeId = useFloatingNodeId();
   221	  const { rootRef, nested } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
   222	
   223	  const { open } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
   224	
   225	  const state: NavigationMenuRoot.State = React.useMemo(
   226	    () => ({
   227	      open,
   228	      nested,
   229	    }),
   230	    [open, nested],
   231	  );
   232	
   233	  const element = useRenderElement(nested ? 'div' : 'nav', props.componentProps, {
   234	    state,
   235	    ref: [props.forwardedRef, rootRef],
   236	    props: [{ 'aria-orientation': orientation }, elementProps],
   237	  });
   238	
   239	  return (
   240	    <NavigationMenuTreeContext.Provider value={nodeId}>
   241	      {element}
   242	    </NavigationMenuTreeContext.Provider>
   243	  );
   244	}

   246	export namespace NavigationMenuRoot {
   247	  export interface State {
   248	    /**
   249	     * If `true`, the popup is open.
   250	     */
   251	    open: boolean;
   252	    /**
   253	     * Whether the navigation menu is nested.
   254	     */
   255	    nested: boolean;
   256	  }
   257	
   258	  export interface Props extends BaseUIComponentProps<'nav', State> {
   259	    /**
   260	     * A ref to imperative actions.
   261	     */
   262	    actionsRef?: React.RefObject<Actions>;
   263	    /**
   264	     * Event handler called after any animations complete when the navigation menu is closed.
   265	     */
   266	    onOpenChangeComplete?: (open: boolean) => void;
   267	    /**
   268	     * The controlled value of the navigation menu item that should be currently open.
   269	     * When non-nullish, the menu will be open. When nullish, the menu will be closed.
   270	     *
   271	     * To render an uncontrolled navigation menu, use the `defaultValue` prop instead.
   272	     * @default null
   273	     */
   274	    value?: any;
   275	    /**
   276	     * The uncontrolled value of the item that should be initially selected.
   277	     *
   278	     * To render a controlled navigation menu, use the `value` prop instead.
   279	     * @default null
   280	     */
   281	    defaultValue?: any;
   282	    /**
   283	     * Callback fired when the value changes.
   284	     */
   285	    onValueChange?: (
   286	      value: any,
   287	      event: Event | undefined,
   288	      reason: BaseOpenChangeReason | undefined,
   289	    ) => void;
   290	    /**
   291	     * How long to wait before opening the navigation menu. Specified in milliseconds.
   292	     * @default 50
   293	     */
   294	    delay?: number;
   295	    /**
   296	     * How long to wait before closing the navigation menu. Specified in milliseconds.
   297	     * @default 50
   298	     */
   299	    closeDelay?: number;
   300	    /**
   301	     * The orientation of the navigation menu.
   302	     * @default 'horizontal'
   303	     */
   304	    orientation?: 'horizontal' | 'vertical';
   305	  }
   306	
   307	  export interface Actions {
   308	    /**
   309	     * When specified, the navigation menu will not be unmounted when closed.
   310	     * Instead, the `unmount` function must be called to unmount the navigation menu manually.
   311	     * Useful when the navigation menu's animation is controlled by an external library.
   312	     */
   313	    unmount: () => void;
   314	  }
   315	}

    40	  const {
    41	    open,
    42	    transitionStatus,
    43	    popupElement,
    44	    positionerElement,
    45	    setPopupElement,
    46	    beforeInsideRef,
    47	    beforeOutsideRef,
    48	    afterInsideRef,
    49	    afterOutsideRef,
    50	  } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
    51	  const positioning = useNavigationMenuPositionerContext();
    52	  const direction = useDirection();
    53	
    54	  const id = useBaseUiId(idProp);
    55	
    56	  const state: NavigationMenuPopup.State = React.useMemo(
    57	    () => ({
    58	      open,
    59	      transitionStatus,
    60	      side: positioning.side,
    61	      align: positioning.align,
    62	      anchorHidden: positioning.anchorHidden,
    63	    }),
    64	    [open, transitionStatus, positioning.side, positioning.align, positioning.anchorHidden],
    65	  );
    66	
    67	  // Allow the arrow to transition while the popup's size transitions.
    68	  useIsoLayoutEffect(() => {
    69	    if (!popupElement || typeof ResizeObserver === 'undefined') {
    70	      return undefined;
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    const observer = new ResizeObserver((entries) => {
    74	      positioning.update();
    75	      if (entries.length > 0 && open) {
    76	        const entry = entries[0];
    77	        // Use offsetWidth/Height to include context of padding/border if necessary, 
    78	        // but contentRect is usually what's used for sizing.
    79	        // Actually, trigger uses offsetWidth/Height.
    80	        const width = (entry.target as HTMLElement).offsetWidth;
    81	        const height = (entry.target as HTMLElement).offsetHeight;
    82	
    83	        const currentWidthVar = popupElement.style.getPropertyValue(
    84	          NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupWidth,
    85	        );
    86	        const currentHeightVar = popupElement.style.getPropertyValue(
    87	          NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupHeight,
    88	        );
    89	        if (
    90	          currentWidthVar &&
    91	          currentWidthVar !== 'auto' &&
    92	          currentHeightVar &&
    93	          currentHeightVar !== 'auto'
    94	        ) {
    95	          popupElement.style.setProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupWidth, `${width}px`);
    96	          popupElement.style.setProperty(NavigationMenuPopupCssVars.popupHeight, `${height}px`);
    97	        }
    98	      }
    99	    });
   100	    observer.observe(popupElement);
   101	    return () => {
   102	      observer.disconnect();
   103	    };
   104	  }, [popupElement, positioning.update, open]);
   105	
   106	
   107	
   108	  // Ensure popup size transitions correctly when anchored to `bottom` (side=top) or `right` (side=left).
   109	  let isOriginSide = positioning.side === 'top';
   110	  let isPhysicalLeft = positioning.side === 'left';
   111	  if (direction === 'rtl') {
   112	    isOriginSide = isOriginSide || positioning.side === 'inline-end';
   113	    isPhysicalLeft = isPhysicalLeft || positioning.side === 'inline-end';
   114	  } else {
   115	    isOriginSide = isOriginSide || positioning.side === 'inline-start';
   116	    isPhysicalLeft = isPhysicalLeft || positioning.side === 'inline-start';
   117	  }
   118	
   119	  const element = useRenderElement('nav', componentProps, {
   120	    state,
   121	    ref: [forwardedRef, setPopupElement],
   122	    props: [
   123	      {
   124	        id,
   125	        tabIndex: -1,
   126	        style: isOriginSide
   127	          ? {
   128	              position: 'absolute',
   129	              [positioning.side === 'top' ? 'bottom' : 'top']: '0',
   130	              [isPhysicalLeft ? 'right' : 'left']: '0',
   131	            }
   132	          : {},
   133	      },
   134	      elementProps,
   135	    ],
   136	    customStyleHookMapping,
   137	  });
   138	
   139	  return (
   140	    <React.Fragment>
   141	      <FocusGuard
   142	        ref={beforeInsideRef}
   143	        onFocus={(event) => {
   144	          if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   145	            getNextTabbable(positionerElement)?.focus();
   146	          } else {
   147	            beforeOutsideRef.current?.focus();
   148	          }
   149	        }}
   150	      />
   151	      {element}
   152	      <FocusGuard
   153	        ref={afterInsideRef}
   154	        onFocus={(event) => {
   155	          if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   156	            getPreviousTabbable(positionerElement)?.focus();
   157	          } else {
   158	            afterOutsideRef.current?.focus();
   159	          }
   160	        }}
   161	      />
   162	    </React.Fragment>
   163	  );
   164	});
   165	
   166	export namespace NavigationMenuPopup {
   167	  export interface State {
   168	    /**
   169	     * If `true`, the popup is open.
   170	     */
   171	    open: boolean;
   172	    /**
   173	     * The transition status of the popup.
   174	     */
   175	    transitionStatus: TransitionStatus;
   176	  }
   177	
   178	  export interface Props extends BaseUIComponentProps<'nav', State> {}
   179	}
   180

   103	    if (!popupElement) {
   104	      return;
   105	    }

   138	      sizeFrame2.request(() => {

   233	  function handleOpenChange(
   234	    nextOpen: boolean,

   241	      return;

   267	      }

   270	
   271	    function changeState() {
   272	      if (isHover) {
   273	        // Only allow "patient" clicks to close the popup if it's open.
   274	        // If they clicked within 500ms of the popup opening, keep it open.
   275	        setStickIfOpen(true);
   276	        stickIfOpenTimeout.clear();
   277	        stickIfOpenTimeout.start(PATIENT_CLICK_THRESHOLD, () => {

   291	    } else {

   293	    }

   295

   317	  const dismiss = useDismiss(context, {

   319	    outsidePress(event) {
   320	      // When pressing a new trigger with touch input, prevent closing the popup.
   321	      const target = getTarget(event) as HTMLElement | null;

   332	  }, [isActiveItem, context, setFloatingRootContext, prevTriggerElementRef, triggerElement]);
   333	
   334	  const { getReferenceProps } = useInteractions([hover, click, dismiss]);
   335	
   336	  const handleOpenEvent = useEventCallback((event: React.MouseEvent | React.KeyboardEvent) => {
   337	    if (!popupElement) {
   338	      return;
   339	    }
   340	
   341	    const currentWidth = popupElement.offsetWidth;
   342	    const currentHeight = popupElement.offsetHeight;
   343	
   344	    ReactDOM.flushSync(() => {
   345	      const prevTriggerRect = prevTriggerElementRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
   346	
   347	      if (mounted && prevTriggerRect && triggerElement) {
   348	        const nextTriggerRect = triggerElement.getBoundingClientRect();
   349	        const isMovingRight = nextTriggerRect.left > prevTriggerRect.left;
   350	        const isMovingDown = nextTriggerRect.top > prevTriggerRect.top;
   351	
   352	        if (orientation === 'horizontal' && nextTriggerRect.left !== prevTriggerRect.left) {
   353	          setActivationDirection(isMovingRight ? 'right' : 'left');
   354	        } else if (orientation === 'vertical' && nextTriggerRect.top !== prevTriggerRect.top) {
   355	          setActivationDirection(isMovingDown ? 'down' : 'up');
   356	        }
   357	      } else if (mounted && !prevTriggerRect && triggerElement) {
   358	        setActivationDirection(null);
   359	      }
   360	
   361	
   362	      // Reset the `openEvent` to `undefined` when the active item changes so that a
   363	      // `click` -> `hover` on new trigger -> `hover` back to old trigger doesn't unexpectedly
   364	      // cause the popup to remain stuck open when leaving the old trigger.
   365	      if (event.type !== 'click') {
   366	        context.dataRef.current.openEvent = undefined;
   367	      }
   368	
   369	      if (pointerType === 'touch' && event.type !== 'click') {
   370	        return;
   371	      }
   372	
   373	      if (value != null) {
   374	        setValue(
   375	          itemValue,
   376	          event.nativeEvent,
   377	          event.type === 'mouseenter' ? 'trigger-hover' : 'trigger-press',
   378	        );
   379	      }
   380	    });
   381	
   382	    handleValueChange(currentWidth, currentHeight);
   383	  });
   384	
   385	  const state: NavigationMenuTrigger.State = React.useMemo(
   386	    () => ({
   387	      open: isActiveItem,
   388	    }),
   389	    [isActiveItem],
   390	  );
   391	
   392	  function handleSetPointerType(event: React.PointerEvent) {
   393	    setPointerType(event.pointerType);
   394	  }
   395	
   396	  const defaultProps: HTMLProps = {
   397	    tabIndex: 0,
   398	    onMouseEnter: handleOpenEvent,
   399	    onClick: handleOpenEvent,
   400	    onPointerEnter: handleSetPointerType,
   401	    onPointerDown: handleSetPointerType,
   402	    'aria-expanded': isActiveItem,
   403	    'aria-controls': isActiveItem ? popupElement?.id : undefined,
   404	    [TRIGGER_IDENTIFIER as string]: '',
   405	    onMouseMove() {
   406	      allowFocusRef.current = false;
   407	    },
   408	    onKeyDown(event) {
   409	      allowFocusRef.current = true;
   410	      const openHorizontal = orientation === 'horizontal' && event.key === 'ArrowDown';
   411	      const openVertical = orientation === 'vertical' && event.key === 'ArrowRight';
   412	
   413	      if (openHorizontal || openVertical) {
   414	        setValue(itemValue, event.nativeEvent, 'list-navigation');
   415	        handleOpenEvent(event);
   416	        stopEvent(event);
   417	      }
   418	    },
   419	    onBlur(event) {
   420	      if (
   421	        event.relatedTarget &&
   422	        isOutsideMenuEvent(
   423	          {
   424	            currentTarget: event.currentTarget,
   425	            relatedTarget: event.relatedTarget as HTMLElement | null,
   426	          },
   427	          { popupElement, rootRef, tree, nodeId },
   428	        )
   429	      ) {
   430	        setValue(null, event.nativeEvent, 'focus-out');
   431	      }
   432	    },
   433	  };
   434	
   435	  const { getButtonProps, buttonRef } = useButton({
   436	    disabled,
   437	    focusableWhenDisabled: true,
   438	    native: nativeButton,
   439	  });
   440	
   441	  return (
   442	    <React.Fragment>
   443	      <CompositeItem
   444	        tag="button"
   445	        render={render}
   446	        className={className}
   447	        state={state}
   448	        customStyleHookMapping={pressableTriggerOpenStateMapping}
   449	        refs={[forwardedRef, setTriggerElement, buttonRef]}
   450	        props={[getReferenceProps, defaultProps, elementProps, getButtonProps]}
   451	      />
   452	      {isActiveItem && (
   453	        <React.Fragment>
   454	          <FocusGuard
   455	            ref={beforeOutsideRef}
   456	            onFocus={(event) => {
   457	              if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   458	                beforeInsideRef.current?.focus();
   459	              } else {
   460	                const prevTabbable = getPreviousTabbable(triggerElement);
   461	                prevTabbable?.focus();
   462	              }
   463	            }}
   464	          />
   465	          <span aria-owns={popupElement?.id} style={visuallyHidden} />
   466	          <FocusGuard
   467	            ref={afterOutsideRef}
   468	            onFocus={(event) => {
   469	              if (positionerElement && isOutsideEvent(event, positionerElement)) {
   470	                afterInsideRef.current?.focus();
   471	              } else {
   472	                const nextTabbable = getNextTabbable(triggerElement);
   473	                nextTabbable?.focus();
   474	
   475	                if (!contains(rootRef.current, nextTabbable)) {
   476	                  setValue(null, event.nativeEvent, 'focus-out');
   477	                }
   478	              }
   479	            }}
   480	          />
   481	        </React.Fragment>
   482	      )}
   483	    </React.Fragment>
   484	  );
   485	});
   486	
   487	export namespace NavigationMenuTrigger {
   488	  export interface State {
   489	    /**
   490	     * If `true`, the popup is open and the item is active.
   491	     */
   492	    open: boolean;
   493	  }
   494	
   495	  export interface Props extends NativeButtonProps, BaseUIComponentProps<'button', State> {}
   496	}
   497

    34	 * A container for the content of the navigation menu item that is moved into the popup
    35	 * when the item is active.
    36	 * Renders a `<div>` element.
    37	 *
    38	 * Documentation: [Base UI Navigation Menu](https://base-ui.com/react/components/navigation-menu)
    39	 */
    40	export const NavigationMenuContent = React.forwardRef(function NavigationMenuContent(
    41	  componentProps: NavigationMenuContent.Props,
    42	  forwardedRef: React.ForwardedRef<HTMLDivElement>,
    43	) {
    44	  const { className, render, ...elementProps } = componentProps;
    45	
    46	  const {
    47	    mounted: popupMounted,
    48	    viewportElement,
    49	    value,
    50	    activationDirection,
    51	    currentContentRef,
    52	    nested,
    53	  } = useNavigationMenuRootContext();
    54	
    55	  const itemValue = useNavigationMenuItemContext();
    56	  const nodeId = useNavigationMenuTreeContext();
    57	
    58	  const open = popupMounted && value === itemValue;
    59	
    60	  const ref = React.useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
    61	
    62	  const [focusInside, setFocusInside] = React.useState(false);
    63	
    64	  const { mounted, setMounted, transitionStatus } = useTransitionStatus(open);
    65	
    66	  useOpenChangeComplete({
    67	    ref,
    68	    open,
    69	    onComplete() {
    70	      if (!open) {
    71	        setMounted(false);
    72	      }
    73	    },
    74	  });
    75	
    76	  const state: NavigationMenuContent.State = React.useMemo(
    77	    () => ({
    78	      open,
    79	      transitionStatus,
    80	      activationDirection,
    81	    }),
    82	    [open, transitionStatus, activationDirection],
    83	  );
    84	
    85	  const handleCurrentContentRef = React.useCallback(
    86	    (node: HTMLDivElement | null) => {
    87	      if (node) {
    88	        currentContentRef.current = node;
    89	      }
    90	    },
    91	    [currentContentRef],
    92	  );
    93	
    94	  const commonProps: HTMLProps = {
    95	    onFocus() {
    96	      setFocusInside(true);
    97	    },
    98	    onBlur(event) {
    99	      if (!contains(event.currentTarget, event.relatedTarget)) {
   100	        setFocusInside(false);
   101	      }
   102	    },
   103	  };
   104

   106	    !open && mounted
   107	      ? {
   108	          style: { position: 'absolute', top: 0, left: 0 },

   110	          ...commonProps,
   111	        }

   118	  }
